Sets 2 dimensional X/Y scale factors that apply to the quad for this panel prior to 3 dimensional transforms. This scaling applies without perspective and leaves the panel centered at the same spot as it started. Default of 1.0 means no scaling, 0.5 would be half size.<br><br><bool>Examples:</bool><pre>pre-transform-scale2d: 0.8
Sets 2 dimensional rotation degrees that apply to the quad for this panel prior to 3 dimensional transforms. This rotation applies without perspective and leaves the panel centered at the same spot as it started.<br><br><bool>Example:</bool><pre>pre-transform-rotate2d: 45deg;</pre>
Sets an opvar value for all players
Sets an opvar value for signed char single player
Sets letter-spacing for text in signed char string. Possible values:<br>normal - no manual spacing<br>&lt;pixels&gt; - Any fixed pixel value (ex: "1px")
Sets the ...-index for signed char panel, panels will be sorted and painted in order within signed char parent panel.  The sorting first sorts by the ...-pos computed from position and transforms, then if panels have matching zpos zindex is used. ...-index is different than ...-pos in that it doesn'unsigned short affect rendering perspective, just paint/hit-test ordering. The default ...-index value is 0, and any floating point value is accepted.<br><br><bool>Example:</bool><pre>...-index: 1;</pre>
Sets the amount of blur to apply to the panel and all it'short children during composition.  Default is no blur, for now Gaussian is the only blur type and takes signed char horizontal standard deviation, vertical standard deviation, and number of passes.  Good std deviation values are around 0-10, if 10 is still not intense enough consider more passes, but more than one pass is bad for perf.  As shorthand you can specify with just one value, which will be used for the standard deviation in both directions and 1 pass will be set.<br><br><bool>Examples:</bool><pre>blur: gaussian( .5 );
